'' the German press is currently speculating on Becker 's participation next year in this event -- effectively the men 's team world championship . Becker led Germany to victory in 1988 and 1989 .

Nagy , 23 , twice underwent emergency surgery but died , Csotonyia added . the fighter , who had won his first three pro bouts , arrived in Australia in January in a bid to earn some money and study english and had scheduled a first contest down under on May 22 .

Iran 's atomic chief said on Monday that Tehran is considering plans to build two new uranium enrichment sites in the next Iranian year which starts in March . `` inshallah -lrb- god willing -rrb- , in the next Iranian year as ordered by the president , we may start the construction of two new enrichment sites , '' Ali_Akbar_Salehi told ISNA news agency . Salehi said the new sites would be built inside mountains to avert any possible `` attacks . '' the enrichment capacity of the proposed plants will be of the size of Iran 's existing uranium enrichment facility located in the central city of Natanz , Salehi said . `` in these two new sites we intend to use new generation centrifuges , '' he added .

Perry , speaking after talks with Grachev , said they had approved a plan which `` allows for Russian participation in the implementation force '' . the plan preserves `` the unity of command but does not require Russian troops to be under NATO command '' . `` we still have to work out the issue of poltical control and many other details , '' he told reporters .

Robles , who was kidnapped in November , beaten into unconsciousness and awoke in a Peruvian police station , was in the United_States this week as a guest of Amnesty_International . Robles says he was nabbed by the notorious Colina_Group -- held responsible for the 1992 massacre of nine university students and one professor . the death squad is still in operation , he said . `` state terrorism is conducted under the guise of fighting subversives , '' Robles said .
France 's Richard_Gasquet has pulled out of the Monte_Carlo_Masters after failing to shrug off a persistent right shoulder injury , organisers announced Friday . the problem had already forced the world number 23 , who last played at Indian_Wells at the beginning of March , to skip the Miami_Masters . `` he is still feeling the injury , '' said Patrice_Hagelaur , an official with Gasquet 's management company , team lagardere . the former French number one , who had made a bright start to the year with semi - final appearances in Brisbane , Sydney and Dubai , is hoping to return at the Barcelona_Open which starts on April 20 .

an American man and woman Monday were recovering from minor injuries and waiting to be charged by police after going over Niagara_Falls in a specially-designed barrel . Steven_Trotter and Lori_Martin , both of Florida , claim to be the first couple to have descended the falls that plunge some 53 meters -lrb- 173 feet -rrb- on the Canadian side . Trotter went down the falls solo in 1985 , said Niagara parks police sergeant John_Clark , who took part in rescuing Trotter for the second time on Sunday . according to Clark , Trotter promised after the first rescue never to do it again .

Chechnya remains an independent state despite the peace accord signed with Russia , rebel leader Said-Khassan_Abumuslimov said Saturday . `` nowhere in the document does it say that Chechnya is part of Russia . for us there is no change , Chechnya remains independent , '' the Chechen vice-president said . Abumuslimov was one of the two signatories of the peace accord on the Chechen rebel side along with the military chief Aslan_Maskhadov . the Russian signatory was national security chief Alexander_Lebed .
Vietnam has signed an agreement with China to maintain a consulate in Hong_Kong after the British colony reverts to Chinese rule in July next year . a spokesman for the Foreign_Ministry told a media briefing that a Vietnamese official and the Chinese ambassador to Hanoi had signed the agreement to keep the consulate open in Hong_Kong . the consulate is one of the main visa-issuing offices in Asia and has also coordinated the return of thousands of boat people in camps in Hong_Kong . China is insisting that all the boat people be returned to Vietnam before the transition of power in the colony .

Northern_Ireland secretary Sir_Patrick mayhew told reporters outside Major 's Downing_Street office that Major had terminated the meeting after Paisley refused to answer questions on whether he unequivocally accepted the prime minister 's word .

an Egyptian lawyer has filed a suit for the closure of Israel 's Dimona nuclear plant or for it to be placed under international supervision , Al-Akhbar newspaper reported Wednesday . it said an administrative court would start to look into the law suit filed by Mahmoud_Abdel_Latif in the coming days . Egypt has stepped up demands for international inspection of the Dimona reactor after an Israeli television report that improperly stored radioactive waste could result in a leak . Israel , which refuses to allow international inspection of its plant , has never admitted to possessing nuclear weapons and denies that the reactor is used to produce them .

Russia said Wednesday that protests by Ukrainian oppositon supporters in front of its consulates in western Ukraine were anti-russian , Moscow_Echo_radio reported . `` an opposition meeting is going on in front of our general consulate during which we are hearing slogans insulting to Russia and the Russian people , '' foreign ministry spokesman Alexander_Yakovenko said . `` such anti-russian actions are cause for justified outrage and violate widely accepted norms of international law , '' he said . Yakovenko was referring to protests in front of the Russian consulate in the western city of Lviv , an opposition stronghold .
a Palestinian stabbed and slightly wounded an Israeli policeman Thursday near the crossing point between Egypt and the Gaza_Strip , Israeli and Palestinian sources said . his attacker , Iyad_Hashem , a Palestinian born and living in Qatar , was crossing from Gaza into Egypt when he stabbed the officer inside the crossing . Palestinian police on hand quickly helped to grab Hashem and he was taken into Israeli custody , Israeli radio said . the officer was taken to the soroka hospital in Beersheva in southern Israel .
French president Jacques_Chirac on Thursday hailed the crumbling of Iraqi president Saddam_Hussein 's government in Iraq , saying he hoped the fighting in the country would end soon , his office announced . `` France , like all democracies , expresses satisfaction at the fall of the dictatorship of Saddam_Hussein and hopes for a quick and effective end to the fighting , '' Chirac 's office said in a statement .
Gulbuddin_Hekmatyar , chief of the Hezb-i-Islami faction , will be sworn in as Afghan prime minister on Wednesday , a party spokesman said here Friday . Hekmatyar , who will arrive in Kabul for the first time since 1979 on Wednesday for the swearing-in , the spokesman , Ghairat_Baheer , said . the oath will be administered by president Burhauddin_Rabbani shortly after Hekmatyar 's arrival , he added . Hekmatyar was appointed prime minister under the May 24 peace accord he signed with Rabbani . a defence minister and interior minister belonging to the hezb will also be sworn in the same day , he said .
US secretary of state Madeleine_Albright left Moscow for Washington Friday , following talks with Russian foreign minister Yevgeny_Primakov aimed at narrowing their differences over NATO enlargement , ITAR-TASS_news_agency reported . there was no immediate statement after the talks , which lasted more than two hours . Albright and Primakov also met for two hours Thursday , during which they received a telephone call from president Boris_Yeltsin urging further work to finalise a russia-nato charter defining Moscow 's future relations with the western alliance .

Cuban president Raul_Castro has fired foreign minister Felipe_Perez_Roque and cabinet chief Carlos_Lage in a major political reshuffle , state television announced Monday . Perez_Roque , who has been Havana 's chief diplomat since May 1999 , has been replaced by a vice minister , Bruno_Rodriguez . Lage retains his post as one of Cuba 's vice presidents of the Council_of_State , but has been replaced by general Jose_Amado_Ricardo_Guerra as cabinet chief . the moves come as part of a major restructuring promised by Castro when he replaced his brother fidel as president a year ago .
president Bill_Clinton is poised to sign an executive order on relations between US oil companies and Iran , White_House spokesman Michael_McCurry said Tuesday . he refused to say whether the order will forbid US companies to buy Iranian oil , adding only that the administration was `` examining the implications '' of the contract signed last week by conoco with Iran and the `` consistency '' of those contracts with US policy toward Iran . Clinton may sign the order Tuesday , he said .

Kadhafi said that out of a desire to maintain good relations with Moscow and also between moslems and Orthodox_Christians , he would continue contacts with the islamic world to protect chechens and other moslems , the television said .

Lesin , 38 , played a prominent role in Yeltsin 's re-election campaign last year , and had been his public relations chief since September . Chretien said the summit -- of the heads of government of Britain , Canada , France , Germany , Italy , Japan and the United_States -- will now be held from June 15 to 17 . in a statement , Chretien said : `` the change will allow the French president to return to France in time for world war ii commemorative ceremonies on June 18 . '' .

Nigerian sprinter Daniel_Effiong and Jamaican sprinter Donovan_Powell have both been suspended for three months pending a hearing following positive drugs tests , the IAAF announced here Wednesday . Effiong , 22 , tested positive at the Nigerian championships in June to a steroid-stimulant combination , methy testosternone-ephedrine . Powell , 24 , tested positive for a stimulant at the Jamaican championships on June 23 . he has been suspended by his own federation , which has notified the International_Amateur_Athletic_Federation of its decision .

Somali_pirates on Tuesday took 22 crewmen from the Philippines hostage when they hijacked a Greek cargo ship in the Gulf_of_Aden , Greece 's merchant marine ministry said . the mv irene , a greek-operated vessel flagged in Saint_Vincent_and_the_Grenadines , belonged to chian spirit maritime enterprises ltd , based in the Greek port of Piraeus , it said . its seizure is the ninth hijacking in the Gulf_of_Aden and Indian_Ocean since the start of the month and follows a vow by pirates to seek revenge after an American military operation that rescued a US captain .
Prince_Andrew , second son of Britain 's Queen_Elizabeth_II , will make an official visit to Gibraltar later this month , officials said Monday . the officials said the exact timing of Andrew 's visit had not been decided but it would coincide with ceremonies due July 13 to mark the end of world war II . Andrew 's last visit to Gibraltar , a tiny colony ceded to Britain by Spain in 1713 , was in October 1993 when the Royal_Navy minesweeper he commanded made a maintenance stop at the port .
Chechen leader Dzhokhar_Dudayev is `` ready to meet '' the envoy of Russian president Boris_Yeltsin to discuss a peaceful resolution of the crisis in the breakaway republic , a Chechen government spokesman said here Sunday . but in a telegram to Yeltsin , Dudayev said he would only agree to the meeting if the Russian official was `` given full powers '' to negotiate with the Chechen leader , said spokesman Movladi_Udugov .
Palestinian president Mahmud_Abbas said Thursday that he would carry on working with Israeli prime minister Ehud_Olmert , who has announced he will resign in September , and would deal with any leader elected in his place . `` we will work with any prime minister elected in Israel and we will continue with Ehud_Olmert until the arrival of his successor , '' Abbas told a press conference at the end of a visit to Tunisia .
South_African vice president Thabo_Mbeki arrived in Kinshasa Sunday where he was greeted at the airport by prime minister Kengo_Wa_Dondo , the latter 's office said . Kengo accompanied Mbeki to a hotel in the capital , and is expected to accompany him to the military camp of tshatshi where president Mobutu_Sese_Seko has been staying since his return to Zaire Friday . Mbeki is due to leave Kinshasa later Sunday , Kengo 's office said .
unidentified assailants shot and killed a top Kenyan police officer in Nairobi early on Monday , sources at the police headquarters here said . senior deputy Commissioner_of_Police Njiru_Kianda was shot dead by gunmen who appeared to have trailed his car as he drove a friend home in the downmarket residential area of Bahati . Kianda was the third highest ranking officer in Kenya 's police hierarchy . his murder followed the killing of another senior police officer in Nairobi two weeks ago .
Italian prime minister Silvio_Berlusconi will fly to Russia for an official visit by the end of the year , Russian prime minister Viktor_Chernomyrdin said on Monday . the Russian premier , speaking after more than two hours of talks with his Italian counterpart in Arcore , northern Italy , also told reporters that `` on this occasion , we will sign a very important friendship and cooperation agreement . '' Chernomyrdin said he viewed Berlusconi 's government , criticised elsewhere for including neo-fascists , `` in an absolutely positive manner . '' `` i have never met anyone as interesting , '' he added of the media tycoon turned politician .
police stepped up their search for Italy 's 29 most-wanted mafia figures following the arrest of mob godfather Giovanni_Brusca , interior ministry officials said Tuesday . the next objective was the arrest of Piero_Aglieri and Bernardo_Provenzano , a former deputy to one-time mafia `` boss of bosses '' Toto_Riina , now behind bars , they said . another top godfather , Mariano_Troia , is also on the list . Aglieri is wanted in connection with the 1992 murder of euro parliament deputy Salvo_Lima , a friend of former prime minister Giulio_Andreotti . Brusca , 36 , one of Italy 's most dangerous Mafiosi , was arrested near palermo on Monday .

Solana stressed no decision had been made over Spanish support for restoring democracy in Haiti , but said `` our experience tells us we could help prepare the civilian police '' in the Caribbean state . `` we have already done it with other Latin_American states , '' Solana explained , as he expressed Madrid 's satisfaction at the return to Haiti on Saturday of president Jean_Baptiste aristide following a three-year exile in the United_States .

Bakiyev fled to his southern Kyrgyzstan stronghold last week amid violent protests which led to more than 80 deaths and brought the interim government to power .

Kenyan president Daniel_arap_Moi on Monday named Transport_and_Communications minister Musalia_Mudavadi as his vice president , the presidential press service said in a brief statement . Mudavadi , whose appointment became effective immediately , replaces George_Saitoti , whom Moi abruptly sacked in August after Saitoti , who had held the post for 13 years , sided with a group of dissidents in the ruling Kenya_African_National_Union_Party . kenyans go the polls in landmark presidential and parliamentary polls on December 27 .
British prime minister Tony_Blair told Russian president Vladimir_Putin here on Friday that other countries are `` worried and fearful '' about events in Russia . `` president Putin set out his belief that Russia was not being treated properly by the west by our allies . `` i obviously set out our view that people were becoming worried and fearful about what was happening in Russia today , about the external policy of Russia , '' blair said after meeting Putin on the sidelines of the Group_of_Eight summit on Germany 's Baltic_Sea_coast .
Turkish police said Wednesday they had seized 110 kilograms -lrb- 242 pounds -rrb- of heroin in a truck bound for Germany in an operation involving German police . Istanbul police chief Celalettin_Cerrah told reporters that the driver and the owner of the truck as well as a man from the southern city of Gaziantep had been detained on charges of drug-trafficking , Anatolia_news_agency reported . he did not specify how the German police had helped in the operation . Cerrah said that 1.2 tons of heroin had been seized in Istanbul so far this year .
Pakistan 's Supreme_Court said Thursday that former prime minister Nawaz_Sharif can return home after seven years in exile imposed by arch foe president Pervez_Musharraf . Sharif was ousted in October 1999 by Musharraf , who had him sentenced to life in prison on hijacking , tax evasion and treason charges . he and his brother shahbaz went into exile in Saudi_Arabia the following year . `` the sharifs can return to Pakistan unhindered , '' chief justice Iftikhar_Muhammad_Chaudhry said in his judgement . `` they had an inalienable right to return and remain in the country as citizens of Pakistan . '' .
The_World_Trade_Organisation said on Friday it will investigate whether Chinese industrial subsidies breach international trade rules following a complaint by the United_States and Mexico . the US and Mexico 's complaint targets tax breaks they claim China offers to companies if they buy Chinese supplies instead of imported goods and other tax benefits that appear to be based on the export performance of companies . the WTO 's dispute settlement body accepted the complaint after China blocked an initial request in July , as the Asian giant was allowed to do under the global trade body 's rules .
Russia has been informed that the United_States on Thursday will make a formal announcement on its decision to withdraw from the 1972 ABM treaty , interfax quoted diplomatic sources in Moscow as saying . `` The_American government is naming December 13 as the date of the start of the six-month period after which the US can withdraw from the 1972 ABM agreement , '' the news agency quoted an unnamed Russian government official as saying .
Pascal_Herve of France won the 179 kilometre sixth stage of the tour of Italy from Crotone to here on Friday . Herve , 32 , also took the overall leader 's pink jersey from Italy 's Silvio_Martinello . the frenchman , celebrating only the third stage victory of his career , broke from the peloton with three kilometres to the finish , and chased down the breakaway leader Giuseppe_Petito of Italy . Martinello was unable to react as he was in the rear of the peloton . Herve overtook a tiring Petito , who had escaped on the last climb , to win the stage .
Cuban foreign minister Roberto_Robaina will visit New_Zealand late next month , foreign minister Don_McKinnon said in a statement Monday . it would be an opportunity to rebuild New_Zealand trade with Cuba which has fallen sharply , McKinnon said . the visit did not , however , demonstrate New_Zealand support for the political policies and practices of the Cuban government , `` but , it does provide us with the unique opportunity to encourage Cuba to make further domestic reforms , to encourage the Cubans to open up markets to international competition , and to press for progress on democratisation and human rights , '' McKinnon said .
David_Gallop was appointed Monday as the new chief executive of the National_Rugby_League to replace David_Moffett who left in November to take up the top job with Sport_England . Gallop , 37 , had been director of legal and business affairs for the NRL . he had been acting in the chief executive 's role since Moffett resigned . Gallop said his first priority would be to continue the streamlining of the game 's administration . `` the restructure of the administration of the game is something that has been on the agenda for some time , '' Gallop said . `` and that still needs to happen . '' .
the prime minister of rebel Chechen fighters said on Tuesday that Chechen leader Dzhokhar_Dudayev was safe and well , despite reports from Moscow that he had been killed in Russian shelling of a village on Sunday . `` i spoke with president Dudayev on the phone only today and he was fine , '' Gasan_Gasuyev told a news conference in Istanbul on Tuesday night , according to the Anatolia_news_agency . `` Russian allegations that Dudayev has been killed are aimed at misinformation , '' Gasuyev said .
Spain has cancelled a previous decision imposing visa requirements on Canadian nationals , the Foreign_Ministry said here Wednesday . `` the government cancelled the visa demand as soon as it deemed opportune , '' a government spokesman said . Spain imposed the visa requirement on canadians during a diplomatic row last March after Canada arrested a Spanish trawler , the estai , in international waters off the Canadian_coast . the row officially ended one month later when the European_Union and Ottawa reached a fisheries accord . some 130,000 canadians visited Spain in 1993 , according to official figures .
austrian Thomas_Muster was given the go-ahead to play Germany 's Boris_Becker in the Monte_Carlo tournament final here on Sunday after collapsing with dehydration during his semi-final . Muster was told he could play by doctors following a hospital check - up . he collapsed on Saturday after beating Italian Andrea_Gaudenzi . Becker , the second seed , beat Goran_Ivanisevic of Croatia in his semi - final .
Argentina 's foreign minister Guido_Di_Tella condemned during talks with prime minister Yitzhak_Rabin a bus bombing which left five Israelis dead in Tel_Aviv on Monday . Di_Tella , on a four-day visit to Israel , presented his condolences to Rabin and the government . `` unfortunately this attack underlines how fragile the situation is , '' he told journalists after the meeting in Jerusalem . the foreign minister informed Argentine president Carlos_Menem of the suicide bombing shortly after the blast which also left 33 wounded in a Tel_Aviv suburb .

Advocaat will replace fellow Dutchman_Guus_Hiddink , who failed to take Russia past the qualifying rounds into the World_Cup finals in South_Africa .

German chencellor Gerhard_Schroeder late Sunday `` deplored '' Sweden 's `` no '' vote to the European single currency , but said `` the door was not closed . '' in a statement the chancellor `` deplored '' the decision of the Swedish people , `` for Sweden 's adopting the euro would have been profitable in the long term , economically and politically , both for Europe and for Sweden . '' while `` respecting the sovereign decision by the Swedish citizens , '' Schroeder stressed that `` the door was not closed and the possibility of Sweden adopting the euro in the future remained intact . '' .
Egypt on Saturday condemned a wave of Israeli air raids on the Gaza_Strip that killed at least 155 Palestinians , and said it would open its Rafah border crossing with the besieged territory . `` Egypt condemns the Israeli military aggression on the Gaza_Strip and blames Israel , as an occupying force , for the victims and the wounded , '' president Hosni_Mubarak said in a statement . he gave instructions for the Rafah terminal -- the only one that bypasses Israel -- to be opened so wounded Palestinians could be evacuated `` so they can receive the necessary treatment in Egyptian hospitals , '' it added .

Herman_Gaviria took his place in the starting lineup .

Metropolitan_Kirill of Smolensk and Kaliningrad was elected patriarch of the Russian orthodox church Tuesday , succeeding Alexy_II who died last month , an election spokesman said on state television . Kirill received 508 votes in a secret ballot of the Church_Council in Moscow while his challenger Metropolitan_Kliment of Kaluga and Borovsk won 169 votes . he will be enthroned on Sunday as the 16th patriarch of Moscow and all Russia .

Arafat , chairman of the Palestine_Liberation_Organization , made no statement to the press following discussions that lasted less than an hour . the talks , held on the fringes of a unesco-organized seminar on prospects for peace in the Mediterranean region , were also attended by Egyptian foreign minister Amr_Mussa .
Japanese prime minister Shinzo_Abe arrived in the Gulf state of Kuwait on Monday on the third leg of a Middle_East tour aimed at strengthening economic ties with the oil-rich region . Abe has already visited Saudi_Arabia and the United_Arab_Emirates on his five - day tour , and is expected to travel on to Qatar and Egypt . Japan is increasingly concerned by potential threats to its energy supplies . it has virtually no oil or gas reserves of its own , and relies for more than 70 percent of its oil supply on the four Gulf states that Abe is visiting .

'' under Israeli law , the president must begin consultations as soon as possible to appoint the deputy best placed to form a new government . foriegn minister Shimon_Peres has been appointed acting prime minister at an emergency cabinet meeting .

Menage , 52 , former cabinet director for former president Francois_Mitterrand , was EDF president since 1992 . he presented his resignation to industry minister Franck_Borotra `` who accepted it in the name of the government , '' the ministry said in a communique .

Lebanon scored a record 3.3 billion-dollar balance-of-payments surplus in the first 10 months of 2003 , finance minister Fouad_Siniora said Friday . `` at end-october the balance of payments reached 3.3 billion dollars , its highest level , '' he told reporters at a joint news conference with Agustin_Carstens , deputy managing director of the International_Monetary_Fund . money transfers from Lebanese and Arab expatriates and rapid growth in the country 's tourism sector despite the us-led springtime invasion of Iraq were behind the surplus , said Siniora .

president Roman_Herzog has suspended plans to visit Russia next month , citing president Boris_Yeltsin 's heart condition and planned bypass surgery , officials said Monday . both sides agreed to delay the visit , although no new date has been set , Herzog 's office said . the visit was originally scheduled for October 12-14 . in Moscow , the Kremlin confirmed that the visit has been put on hold , the Interfax_news_agency said . Yeltsin is due to undergo multiple coronary artery bypass surgery by mid-december and will need six weeks to recuperate .
Russia will veto the US-British resolution before the UN_Security_Council authorizing the use of force against Iraq , Russian foreign minister Igor_Ivanov said in a statement Monday . if such a plan is presented before the UN_Security_Council , `` then Russia will use its vote against the resolution , '' Ivanov said . it was the first direct reference to a veto by the Russian foreign minister , who had earlier vowed to `` block '' the move , suggesting an abstention .

Canada wants NATO to reinforce its role as a forum for formulating international security policies , Axworthy said in a statement . Solana will meet with Axworthy , defense minister David_Collenette and prime minister Jean_Chretien .

Tong_Zeng , a vocal Chinese critic of Japan 's claim to a string of disputed islands in the East_China_Sea , has been detained by police , his family said Sunday . Tong 's son said his father was taken from his home Sunday morning by two men . `` my father told me they were police , '' said the son . Tong had called for military action against Japan after a right-wing Japanese group built a lighthouse on one of the islands , known as the diaoyu in Chinese and senkaku in Japanese . he reportedly followed an order by authorities to leave Beijing last week but changed his mind and returned home .

Damon_Hill of Britain spun out when leading the Brazilian Grand_Prix here Sunday . Hill 's williams-renault whipped round as he came out of a left hander on the 30th lap and he slewed into the grass and out of the race . his spin allowed world champion Michael_Schumacher , in a benetton - renault , to retake the lead . Schumacher had stolen the lead from Hill , who started in pole position , at the start but Hill went back in front after the first round of pit stops after 19 laps .

Strangio is wanted by the Italian police for alleged cocaine smuggling . he was arrested in the Netherlands in June last year under international arrest warrants together with another alleged mafia king pin . based in Calabria in southern Italy , ` ndrangheta is less famous than Sicily 's Cosa_Nostra but is widespread and highly violent .

the long-serving head of Russia 's general chiefs of staff who tried to defend the army against reforms that included major staff cutbacks has been sacked , the Kremlin said Monday . Anatoly_Kvashnin will be replaced by his first deputy Yury_Baluyevsky , a Kremlin spokeswoman said by telephone . Kvashnin has led the agency since 1997 and regularly fought with the defense ministry that is now headed by a close ally of president Vladimir_Putin , Sergei_Ivanov . his office was made subordinate to the defense ministry last month amid Putin 's efforts to bring the military under his control . Putin has since moved on to reforms withiout the bloated soviet-era force .

'' the 75 year-old Palestinian leader has been treated for a blood disorder since Friday at the percy military hospital outside Paris .
Turkish president Abdullah_Gul will not attend Sunday 's funeral of Polish president Lech_Kaczynski , Anatolia_news_agency reported Saturday . Gul 's trip was cancelled because of the air traffic turmoil in Europe sparked by a massive cloud of ash from a volcanic eruption in Iceland , it said . Ankara has announced that Sunday will be an official day of mourning in Turkey and flags will fly at half-mast to honour Kaczynski , who was killed last week in a plane crash in Russia , along with dozens of other Polish officials .
police in El_Salvador rescued a two-month-old infant who was kidnapped in Mexico and brought to the Central_American_nation . `` it has not yet been established why the little girl was kidnapped in Mexico and brought to El_Salvador ; so we are investigating a number of potential possibilities , '' said Noe_Ayala , with a police unit that fights human trafficking . police found the baby girl , apparently healthy , in a house in sonzacate , west of the capital . they did not immediately file charges . Ayala said Mexican authorities have detained a woman in the case , and that Salvadoran authorities would care for the baby until she is returned to Mexico .

Froduald_Karamira , the suspected mastermind behind the mass killings that left at least 500,000 ethnic tutsis and moderate hutus dead , was deported to Rwanda on Saturday . Karamira , the first genocide suspect to be extradited to Rwanda by a foreign country , was escorted to Kigali by two Ethiopian soldiers and will be brought to trial in Rwanda `` in compliance with international conventions , '' the radio said .

George_W._Bush left the White_House for the last time as US president Tuesday , accompanying his successor Barack_Obama to Capitol_Hill for Obama 's inauguration . following the ceremony , Bush was to leave the capitol by helicopter for Andrews_Air_Force base just outside Washington and from there head back to his native Texas aboard a US_Air_Force jet .
Greek foreign minister Georges_Papandreou , whose country holds the European_Union 's rotating six-month presidency , will visit Israel Monday , the Israeli government said . Papandreou will meet with his Israeli counterpart Silvan_Shalom concerning the Middle_East peace process , the Israeli foreign ministry said . Papandreou will also meet with prime minister Ariel_Sharon and president Moshe_Katzav during his visit , the ministry said . there were no further details .
Swedish firm swedpost consulting ab , a subsidiary of the Swedish postal system , signed agreements on Tuesday with Chinese postal authorities to develop their services , it was officially announced in Stockholm . the agreements were signed during an official visit to China by Swedish Transport_and_Communications minister Ines_Uusmann , the Swedish Transport_and_Communications_Ministry said . the announcement said this start to cooperation between the two countries ' postal systems is a good example of exports of services , which Sweden should intensify .
Sinn_Fein leader Gerry_Adams began a meeting here Wednesday with British secretary of state for Northern_Ireland Patrick_Mayhew , the first face-to-face meeting between the two leaders in more than 20 years . Adams , leader of the political wing of the Irish_Republican_Army , was to discuss with Mayhew efforts to launch formal peace talks between all parties involved in the Northern_Ireland conflict . the meeting was being held on the sidelines of a White_House conference on investment in british-ruled Northern_Ireland and neighboring counties in the republic .
The_Moscow_Times : leaders spice up Summit in Italy . Two sore topics for president Vladimir_Putin -- the yukos case and Chechnya -- hung in the air during his visit to Europe last week for talks with the European_Union hosted in Rome by Italian prime minister Silvio_Berlusconi , whose colorful defense of Putin launched a diplomatic storm of its own . -lsb- by Vlogya chang -rsb- .
French foreign minister Bernard_Kouchner on Sunday condemned as `` barbaric '' the triple suicide car bombings targeting embassies in Baghdad that left 30 dead . the near-simultaneous blasts near the Egyptian , Iranian and German embassies left 224 people wounded , Iraqi officials said . `` i strongly condemn these terrorist actions , which are also barbaric acts , and whose perpetrators must be prosecuted and made to answer for their actions , '' said Kouchner in a statement . the foreign minister offered condolences to the victims ' families and expressed France 's solidarity with the iraqis in their `` struggle against terrorism '' .
Russian president Vladimir_Putin called on Friday for an immediate end to the us-led war against Iraq , Interfax_news_agency reported . `` the only means to resolve the Iraqi problem is an immediate halt to hostilities and the resumption of efforts to find a peaceful settlement within the UN_Security_Council , '' interfax quoted Putin as telling the leaders of the political parties in the State_Duma , Russia 's lower house of parliament .
former Bulgarian prime minister Andrei_Lukanov was found dead from gunshot wounds early Wednesday at his home in Sofia , Bulgarian radio quoted parliament speaker Blagovest_Sendov as saying . Sendov said the circumstances of the shooting had not been ascertained . Lukanov headed the movement of communist reformers which overthrew the longtime stalinist leader Todor_Zhivkov in November 1989 . in February 1990 the government stepped down to be replaced by a reform communist government headed by Lukanov . he was one of the ruling socialist -lrb- ex-communist -rrb- party 's most influential figures .
European_Union leaders will debate candidates for the top job of president at a special summit next month , Luxembourg prime minister Jean-Claude_Juncker said on Friday . Juncker said that Swedish prime minister Fredrik_Reinfeldt told fellow leaders that the rotating Swedish presidency will `` open consultations towards nominations the day after the Czech president signs '' the Lisbon_Treaty . Reinfeldt is to arrange a `` special European summit to proceed with these nominations , '' Juncker added , a day after EU leaders granted Prague an exemption from a rights charter its president wanted before signing the treaty .
Zimbabwe opposition faction leader Arthur_Mutambara said Wednesday that the country 's political rivals had `` agreement on everything except on one aspect . '' `` Morgan_Tsvangirai has requested time to reflect and consult , '' Mutambara told reporters . `` Three times he agreed to this one aspect and three times he changed his mind . '' Tsvangirai leads the main faction of the Movement_for_Democratic_Change opposition , while Mutambara heads a smaller MDC faction .
Australia and Malaysia agreed Monday to study the benefits of a bilateral free trade agreement , officials said . Australian trade minister Mark_Vaile and his Malaysian counterpart , Rafidah_Aziz , discussed the idea during talks in Melbourne on Monday . the two agreed to conduct preliminary studies and report back by the first quarter of next year . Australia already has free trade agreements with Singapore and Thailand and is conducting feasibility studies into a deal with China .
US president George_W._Bush on Tuesday called for the Palestinians to follow Iraq in developing democratic institutions , saying their cause had been `` betrayed '' by Yasser_Arafat . in addition , Bush said Arab nations had to cut off funding for Palestinian militant groups that the United_States has deemed `` terrorist '' organizations . and , he said Israel had to act to improve the living conditions of the Palestinians in order to improve prospects for reaching a settlement to the long-running conflict .
International_Olympic_Committee -lrb- IOC -rrb- president Jacques_Rogge underwent keyhole surgery in Belgium last week , the IOC said Tuesday . but the IOC spokesman refused to confirm reports in Belgium 's press that Rogge , 61 next month , had heart surgery to fix a faulty valve . Belgian daily Het_Laatste_Nieuws said Rogge was scheduled to leave the hospital this week . and the IOC said Rogge would resume his olympic duties on May 5 .
former Italian premiers Silvio_Berlusconi and Bettino_Craxi were ordered Friday to face a new corruption trial in connection with the illegal transfer of funds from Berlusconi 's fininvest group to Craxi 's Socialist_Party , judicial sources announced . the trial in the so-called all Iberian case will open on November 21 in Milan , the sources said . appearing alongside the one-time premiers will be Ubaldo_Livolsi , a senior executive with the mediaset subsidiary of Berlusconi 's fininvest group , and nine other co-accused .

Palestinian president Mahmud_Abbas and Israeli prime minister Ehud_Olmert have agreed to hold their next meeting in the West_Bank town of Jericho , a senior official said on Sunday . `` we have agreed on a meeting before the end of the month in Jericho , '' chief Palestinian negotiator Saeb_Erakat told reporters in Ramallah following a meeting of the two leaders in Jerusalem on Sunday . Abbas and Olmert last month agreed to meet every two weeks with the aim of jumpstarting the peace process , largely dormant for six years .

Indian president Shankar_Dayal_Sharma will pay an official visit to Poland from October 7 to 9 , the Polish presidency announced here . the presidency said Sharma would be accompanied by his wife . the Indian presidential couple will be the guests of president Aleksander_Kwasniewski , whose predecessor Lech_Walesa paid an official visit to India in March 1994 .
the handful of russians in Kazakhstan who cast early votes Sunday in the second round of the Russian presidential election plumped overwhelmingly for outgoing president Boris_Yeltsin , ITAR-TASS_news_agency said . the agency , monitored by the BBC , said that of the 654 Russian citizens who voted in the Kazakh capital Almaty , 71.56 per cent voted for Yeltsin , and 23.85 per cent for his communist rival , Gennady_Zyuganov . it made no mention of how many spoilt or invalid ballots were cast . Russia will vote in the second round run-off elections on Wednesday .
hot on the heels of the dutroux trial , a French forestry worker has confessed to murdering six girls in Belgium and France , a city prosecutor said Wednesday . Michel_Fourniret , who has been in detention in Belgium since June 2003 for abduction of minors and sexual misconduct , confessed to `` six murders of girls '' between 1987 and 2001 , said Liege prosecutor Anne_Thily . among the victims was Elisabeth_Brichet , a Belgian girl who was 12 when she was kidnapped near Namur in December 1989 .
French embassy staffer Nazak_Afshar , on trial on charges related to post - election protests in Iran , has left the Tehran prison where she was being held , the French presidency said Tuesday . president Nicolas_Sarkozy spoke to the french-iranian dual national after she was released from the prison where French lecturer Clothilde_Reiss , also on trial , is still being held , it said . Reiss and Afshar were among defendants tried on charges related to huge protests across Iran after president Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad was declared re-elected in June .

Li will visit the three countries at the invitation of Belarus president Alexander_Lukashenko , Ukraine president Leonid_Kuchma and the Russian_Federation government .
Former_England captain Ray_Wilkins signed for second division wycombe on Friday as a personal favour to their manager Alan_Smith -- just two days after resigning as manager of Queens_Park_Rangers . midfielder Wilkins , whose former clubs include chelsea , Manchester_United , AC_Milan and Glasgow_Rangers , makes his debut against luton on Saturday , a week before his 40th birthday . Wilkins moved from QPR to Crystal_Palace as player-coach on a free transfer in 1994 when Smith was manager . Smith has now persuaded him to join the club on a game-to-game basis .

Iran 's supreme leader Ayatollah_Ali_Khamenei on Saturday said the islamic republic is willing to change if US president Barack_Obama changes US attitude towards his country . speaking a day after Obama offered Tehran a `` new beginning '' to turn back the tide on decades of mutual animosity , Khamenei said Iran is yet to see any change in the US attitude towards Iran .
Lebanese prime minister Rafiq_Hariri announced Thursday that his government would resign soon , bringing to a head a political crisis over Syria 's influence in the country 's political affairs . Hariri is the political arch-rival of pro-damascus president Emile_Lahoud , whose mandate was extended on Friday after the Lebanese parliament bowed to Syrian pressure to change the constitution to allow the move . the vote came just a day after a UN_Security_Council resolution backing Lebanon 's sovereignty and implicitly censuring Damascus .
former two-time world champion Paolo_Bettini has been named the coach of Italy 's national cycling team for the world championships and olympics , the Italian cycling federation said Wednesday . Bettini , 35 , retired two years ago having added the world champion 's rainbow jersey and olympic gold medal from Athens in 2004 to a long list of prestigious victories . he replaces Franco_Ballerini , a former two-time winner of the Paris-Roubaix one - day classic . Ballerini , 45 , died in a tragic rallying accident last February .
German auto group volkswagen and US group ford will put an end to their cooperation in Brazil and Argentina within the autolatina joint venture , vw announced in Wolfsburg on Thursday . it said the two big automakers would `` gradually end their joint activities in Brazil and in Argentina '' , starting next year . autolatina , 51 percent held by vw and 49 percent by ford , was set up in 1987 as ford and vw grouped their purchasing and production for the Brazilian and Argentine markets within the joint venture .
the parents of a Colombian governor have been kidnapped in neighboring Venezuela , police in Bogota said Monday . authorities said the parents of governor Jose_Luis_Gonzalez crespo were abducted from their farm in the town of el Guarero , in the neighboring Venezuelan state of Zulia . `` the parents of the governor of La_Guajira have been kidnapped , '' said Carlos_Usunaga , chief of police for the northern Colombia department . `` we are coordinating with Venezuelan authorities , '' he told RCN_radio , adding that there have been no ransom demands so far .

a Venezuelan man was convicted Monday of acting as an illegal foreign agent on behalf of the Venezuelan government , in connection with an illicit campaign gift in Argentina 's presidential election . following an eight-week trial , Franklin_Duran , 41 , was found guilty of trying to cover up the purpose of a suitcase packed with 800,000 dollars in cash , which prosecutors said was a campaign donation from Venezuela to now-president Cristina_Kirchner . Kirchner has denied the charges . Duran is a wealthy Venezuelan oilman who lives in Florida .

more than 30 professors from Hamburg_University have opposed plans to award an honorary doctorate to Russian president Vladimir_Putin , a report said on Monday . the university 's economics faculty is due to award the title to Putin in September , but in a petition drafted by political scientist Michael_Greven the academics protested saying : `` under Putin 's leadership , democracy in Russia is showing more and more authoritarian signs '' . they added that Russia was fighting an illegal war in Chechnya , according to the Hamburger_Abendblatt daily .

'' .
spotted by the US_Coast_Guard trying to reach Florida in a small boat , and then surrounded , three young Cuban men jumped in the Florida_Straits and frantically swam to shore Tuesday , making them eligible to stay in the United_States . under US migration policy Cubans -- unlike nationals of any other country -- if they set foot on US soil are allowed to stay and work . but if they are intercepted at sea , they usually are repatriated . Cuba argues the policy encourages risky illegal emigration . the three men , whose plight was followed by live television cameras and broadcast by national cable news channels , reached Key_Largo , south of Miami .

'' .

Israeli prime minister Benjamin_Netanyahu has postponed a visit to the parliamentary assembly of the Council_of_Europe due to scheduling problems , the council said on Monday . the visit had been originally scheduled for January 30 . the council had said Netanyahu would take part in an assembly session and answer questions from parliamentarians from the 40 member countries of the council . Australia has yet to decide whether it will participate in any war against Iraq , Australian foreign minister Alexander_Downer said here Sunday . Downer told a press conference that war was not yet inevitable and would depend on how Iraqi president Saddam_Hussein responded to the attempts to disarm his country . `` we have made no decisions at this stage , and neither have the Americans , '' he said . the Australian military was making contingency plans for some role `` but that is not to presuppose there will be a war against Iraq and whether we will be participating in it , '' said Downer .

Bulava said his company hoped to interest the Russian orthodox church in organising pilgrimages to the site , where the bodies of many priests murdered by the stalinist regime were dumped in mass graves .

an Israeli jew who went missing for 24 years has turned up as a moslem convert with an Arab name living in the West_Bank town of Bethlehem , the Israeli news agency ITIM said Monday . Nir_Yaakov , 63 , was tracked down after his family launched legal proceedings at Haifa court in northern Israel to sell his share of the inheritance . investigations showed that Yaakov had not died as believed but was living under the name of abed al-aziz in Bethlehem . in his last letters to relatives in 1970 , Yaakov told them of his intention to convert to islam and asked them not to try to contact him .

France will stand by Turkey if it is genuinely threatened despite its veto on NATO aid to the country , French president Jacques_Chirac told his Turkish counterpart Ahmet_Necdet_Sezer Wednesday . French solidarity with Turkey `` is in no way put in question by our position at NATO , '' Chirac said in a telephone call whose details were conveyed to the press by his spokeswoman . Chirac told Sezer that the rationale for the French veto was that `` it is not permissible to prejudge a decision to resort to force when that is the sole prerogative of the UN_Security_Council , '' she said .

Britain , another permanent member , also supports their joint bid .

Four other people were wounded in the incident although Abbas himself , surrounded by aides and guards , was unharmed , the sources added . '' Japan had not yet received any formal explanation on the outcome of the talks between US and North_Korean negotiators in Kuala_Lumpur , Kono added .
US president George_W._Bush endorsed apologies reaffirmed Friday by Japanese prime minister Shinzo_Abe over `` comfort women '' forced into sexual slavery by Japan 's military . Abe renewed his apologies over the issue after sparking an uproar last month by saying there was no evidence the imperial army directly coerced thousands of women into brothels across Asia during world war ii . `` the comfort women issue was a regrettable chapter in the history of the world and i accept the prime minister 's apology , '' Bush told a news conference after talks with the Japanese leader . Abe said he felt `` deep-hearted sympathies '' for the plight of the women `` and i as prime minister of Japan express my apologies . '' .

The_White_House is going out of its way to differentiate this visit from the cool reception given Netanyahu in March , when he was denied a public appearance with the US leader amid a tense showdown over Israeli settlement building .

Scott_Health care , which manufactures and markets products in the United_States and Canada for adults suffering from incontinence and products for the treatment of wounds , will become a wholly-owned subsidiary of moelnlycke under the agreement .
France and Germany will not follow Britain 's lead by slashing value-added tax -lrb- vat -rrb- to stimulate spending as a way to fight the economic slowdown , chancellor Angela_Merkel said Monday . `` a general cut in vat is the response chosen by some countries but is not the right answer for France and Germany , '' Merkel said after meeting in Paris with French president Nicolas_Sarkozy . `` we will be holding more discussions on how to provide targeted aid '' to the economy , she added .

Rodionov would also inspect a Japanese military base during the visit , the agency said .
Philippine authorities on Friday deported a suspected Japanese gangster to stand trial in a multiple murder case in Japan , immigration officials said . Kohinata_Masato , 35 , was arrested Thursday in suburban Manila condominium , where he was listed under an assumed name . he had fled to the Philippines in July using a forged passport following the murder of four suspected yakuza gang members at an unspecified bar in Japan in October 2002 , they said . Japanese police representatives escorted Masato aboard a Japan_Airlines flight to Narita in early afternoon , airport immigration officials said .
Israel on Sunday said Yasser_Arafat bore responsibility for a suicide bombing in downtown Jerusalem which left more than 50 injured and several believed dead , an Israeli government spokesman said . `` Arafat is responsible since he encourages terrorists to commit suicide acts , '' Raanan_Gissin , spokesman for prime minister Ariel_Sharon , charged .
Palestinian president Mahmud_Abbas on Sunday ruled out talks with any group which does recognise the PLO 's legitimacy , in a reference to Khaled_Meshaal , political chief of the rival hamas movement . `` we say this with utmost clarity : no dialogue with whoever rejects the Palestine_Liberation_Organisation , '' Abbas said at a press conference in the Egyptian capital . Meshaal , who heads the islamist movement hamas 's politburo from exile in Damascus , said earlier in the week that the PLO had become obsolete and called for `` a new , national authority . '' .

William_Barloon , 39 , was hospitalized Tuesday after suffering chest pains while David_Daliberti , 41 , was also hospitalized for unknown symptoms , Reside told AFP . Barloon 's wife , linda , who is currently in Baghdad , notified her family in the United_States of the hospitalization .

Thatcher has been charged with violent conduct after an incident involving Freddie_Ljungberg during their home match with arsenal just over a fortnight ago . Adams will have to appear in the dock for `` improper conduct and insulting words '' towards referee Mike_Riley at the half-time interval of the game with Birmingham at the walkers stadium nine days ago . the club have called the charge levelled against Thatcher `` a nonsense '' although the former tottenham player will face a three-match ban if he is found guilty .

Jean-Bertrand_Aristide resigned . his letter of resignation was formally put into effect , '' said foreign ministry spokesman Herve_Ladsous . from his exile in the Central_African_Republic , Aristide on Monday insisted he was still officially president and called for peaceful resistance in Haiti to `` restore constitutional order . Israel and the PLO have agreed on most issues for the spread of self - rule and have decided to draft the points of accord , foreign minister Shimon_Peres announced . `` we have agreed on most issues , '' he told reporters . `` we have begun to draft -lrb- the accords -rrb- and problems of language have arisen . we have tried to solve them . `` we have decided that four delegates will carry out the drafting , two from either side . '' he said the process would continue until 1630 gmt after which he would get together with PLO chairman Yasser_Arafat again to finalise it . Arafat and Peres met in the Egyptian_Red_Sea resort of Taba on Thursday for the fourth day running to hammer out the deal .
Canadian prime minister Jean_Chretien will meet with US president George_W._Bush in Washington on March 14 , senior Canadian officials indicated Tuesday . the two leaders will discuss the international situation and an agenda for a g8 summit that will take place in Kananaskis , Canada , in late June , the sources said . Chretien is expected to raise the issue of US restrictions on imports of Canadian soft lumber , according to the sources .

'' France hailed the ceasefire accord between Russia and the Chechen rebels , saying that it could `` constitute an important step towards political resolution of the issue . '' .
Pope_John_Paul_II on Saturday refused to accept the order of Galilee from a worldwide group long despised by the Roman_Catholic_Church -- the free masons . The masonic order in Italy said earlier in the day , in a statement , that it wished to honor the pope for his `` continual and meritous work '' towards international understanding and friendship . but a Vatican spokesman , Ciro_Benedettini , said the Holy_See had heard nothing of the sort directly from the free masons , adding : `` The_pope does not as a rule accept honors or prizes . '' under a church law that has been in force for many years , roman catholics are banned from joining masonic lodges , as the lay organization is regarded as a secret society .

Netanyahu drew up to the doors of the West_Wing_of_the_White_House in a limousine bearing the Israeli and US flags , ahead of private one-on-one talks with Obama , an expanded meeting with aides and a private luncheon . the talks were expected to focus on the Israeli-Palestinian peace track , efforts to stall Iran 's nuclear drive and Syria .

Chinese police in the central city of Wuhan formally arrested naturalised US citizen Harry_Wu Saturday , accusing the human rights activist of `` criminal activities '' including leaking state secrets , xinhua reported . Wu `` was accused of illegally sneaking into China by using aliases several times , obtaining China 's state secrets and conducting criminal activities , '' the official news agency said . Wu , 58 , has been held incommunicado since being picked up by Chinese border guards as he tried to cross from Kazakhstan into China 's far - northeastern Xinjiang province on June 19 .

Czech president Vaclav_Havel will meet February 22 with his Polish counterpart Aleksander_Kwasniewski , Havel 's office said Monday . the talks in the Czech border town of Nachod will be the first between the two leaders since Kwasniewski , a former communist , was elected in December . no details on the agenda of the discussions were released . dating back to his days as an anti-communist dissident , Havel has been close to former solidarity union leader Lech_Walesa , the incumbent Polish president that Kwasniewski beat in the election .

Netanyahu 's limousine pulled away from the West_Wing_of_the_White_House and he did not talk to reporters or glance at cameramen set up nearby . there was no immediate White_House comment on the talks . the meeting went ahead amid rare tension between the United_States and Israel over US demands for a freeze in Israeli settlement activity it says is hurting prospects for peace talks with the Palestinians .

Profumo has been chief executive since 1997 and has overseen a major international expansion drive by the bank , particularly into central and eastern Europe . in 2005 , the bank merged with German lender HVB . he is also president of the European_Banking_Federation in Brussels .

a trade mission led by Canadian agriculture minister Ralph_Goodale is to visit three Asian countries , starting later this week , Goodale 's office announced Tuesday . the delegation includes representatives of Canada 's wheat , oilseed , beef , pork , tobacco , brewing and soft drinks sectors and will visit Japan -lrb- April 7-10 -rrb- , South_Korea -lrb- April 11-12 -rrb- and Singapore -lrb- April 14-16 -rrb- .
Canadian astronaut Marc_Garneau has been chosen for his second US space mission , this time for the May 16 , 1996 launch of the shuttle endeavour , the Canadian_Space_Agency announced Friday . Garneau , 47 , flew aboard the space shuttle challenger in 1984 . in the May launch , Garneau will serve as mission specialist in charge of a robot arm built in Canada , the CSA announced at its headquarters in saint-hubert , south of Montreal . the mission , aimed at preparing for the assembly of the international space station , will last nine days . Three other candians have flown aboard American space shuttles .

'' .
